Trust and safety

Carbon markets need public confidence to accelerate. Here’s how Patch helps build it.

Download the whitepaper
“When used with integrity, voluntary carbon markets unlock much-needed financing that can accelerate climate action. Transparency and robust standards are fundamental to these markets delivering this goal, and it is great to see how Patch’s approach to trust and safety can contribute to instilling confidence in the market.”
Lydia Sheldrake
Director of Policy & Partnerships, VCMI

The risk

Carbon markets are developing, testing, and scaling the climate solutions the world needs to rebalance the planet. In this rapidly evolving world, carbon credit buyers need to have confidence their purchases are driving the intended climate impact.

Our approach

Patch delivers confidence to buyers through multiple systems of risk reduction, so they can take bold action to accelerate climate solutions.

01.

Comprehensive integrity review

Every project on the Patch platform passes a comprehensive integrity review based on the latest science and market standards. Our project evaluation process is aligned to ICVCM’s Core Carbon Principles and Article 6 standards. Every project evaluation includes an assessment unique and specific to the project’s type and its nuanced risks and benefits.

02.

Deeper analysis and due diligence

Patch’s platform consolidates project and integrity information from across the voluntary carbon market. Our climate experts then translate it to your specific criteria and sustainability strategy. From assessing climate impact to evaluating risk, no question is too complex for our experienced climate strategy and solutions team.

Bee Hui Yeh, Climate Strategy & Solutions

03.

Risk mitigation strategies

Sometimes the risk of a project not delivering on its climate impact is inevitable. We work with you to proactively mitigate risk by building a diversified carbon credit portfolio with a mix of traditional and nascent technologies. We also reactively mitigate risk with default protection for any projects that are unable to deliver a future credit vintage.

A framework to reduce risk and increase transparency

Read Patch’s full framework for trust and safety, including our complete project acceptance criteria:

  • The first principles that guide our approach
  • Detailed requirements for project acceptance
  • Acceptance criteria checklist for easy reference
  • And much more
Download the whitepaper

An iterative approach to managing risk

We’re constantly improving our trust and safety framework so you can be confident your climate action is based on the latest science and leading standards.
